If enabled the prefab will not be baked into the parent map during map compile, but instead will be dynamically loaded in the game. This requires the target map to be compiled separately. If enabled, transforming this node will transform the target node such that the relative offset is maintained, essentially locking the transform of the two objects together regardless of which one is edited.
